1. References A and B concern reporting by AMBIDDY/1 on
an alleged conspiracy developing in Venezuela among right-wing
members of COPE1 to overthrow the LENOI regime. JNWAVE reviewed
the two reports (references) and is forwarding pertinent
information developed for appropriate use by addressees.
2. Reference A paragraph 2 states AMBIDDY/1 said
Venezuelan Hajor (fnu) *GUTIERREZ (Miami representative for
plotters) commutes between Caracas and Miami, and his telephone
number in Miami is 887-0795.
A. The Miami numerical telephone directory lists the
telephone number 887-0795 for Anselmo *ALVARADO, 550 Falcon
Ave., Miami Springs, Florida. (For additional WAVE info re one
Anselmo ALVARADO, see Reference D.)
B. Reference C reported that a (fmm) GUTIERREZ,
550 Falcon Ave., Miami Springs; telephone: TU 7-0795 (1.e.
same number), was listed in the telephone notebook which
belonged to Major Hasel Ange? WOLIMA Franco when he (MOLINA)
was captured.

company would be a very good thing to be able to
as a fishing cooperative and a farming coopora live-also
to ultimately benefit the area's indigenous population.
All of this, of course, hinges upon two fundamental factors:
Firstly, it depends upon the continued goodwill of General
A-1, which is a very good thing to manage to contribute monico
to the previously mentioned agency, it depends to
a lesser extent upon A-1's ability to forge ahead with the
program. This is'more hinges A-1's financial status
and abilities.

MEMORANDUM FOR THE RECORD
SUBJECT: Telephone Conversation with AMBIDDY-1 1001
1. AMBIDDY-1 telephoned the undersigned and indicated
that he was forced to postpone his projected interview with

Venezuela within ten days for the projected meeting.

overcome a recent spate of rumors surrounding his (Oduber's)

be worth him. He claimed that the U.S. offered no objections

a los lades que le abeçro/sienes que visite bien y seule andr exycilio."sano lango y
affindashejuc del cuello puninente.

las Racio-Pratuallos, vestido de spaciano Cajama.

de my alto jenemagia.

asjes a Costa Rica a través cie la Hapajada de Bolivia en San Jasjimuchas veces, a tem

1. AMBIDDY-1 CONTACTED IN MIAMI BY VEN MAJOR (FNU) GUTIERREZ
CLAIMING HE LOCAL REP FOR GROUP OF PLOTTERS CURRENTLY TRAINING FOR
COUP AGA INST LEONI REGIME. A-1 UNABLE OBTAIN NAMES OTHER THAN COL.
MAETIN PARADA. ACCORDING A-1 :EADER OF PLOT LOCATED IN CARACAS
CONVENT NUESTRA SENORA DE FATIMA OR NUESTRA SENORA DEL ROSARIO.
2. A-1 SAID GUTIERREZ COMMUTES BETWEEN CARA AND MIAMI. TELEPHONE
IN MIAMI 887-0795 (NO GUTIERREZ LISTED MIAMI DIRECTORY WITZ THIS
NUMBER).
3. GUTIERREZ GAVE A-1 FOLLOWING INSTRUCTIONS FOR CONTACTING
LEADER: A-1 SHOULD PROCEED CARA AND CALL DR. (FNU) MORELOS (WHOM A-1
SUSPECTS MAY BE PIPIEST). MORELOS WILL THEN TAKE A-1 TO LEADER.

COPEI LEADER (A-1 UNABLE SUPPLY NAME). PURPORTEDLY GARRISONS IN

NO FORIGN BISIN/CONTROLLED DISSE
2
TDCS DB-
PAGE
2
SECRET
315/03788-65
FOR FINANCIAL AID FOR THE CAMPAIGN OF COLONEL MIGUEL ANGEL PONCIANO
SAHAYOA, THE CANDIDATE OF THE MUN FOR PRESIDENT, AND HE WILL ALSO
URGE RIVERA TO EXERT POLITICAL PRESSURE UPON COLONEL ENRIQUE PERALTA
AZUDRIA, CHIEF OF THE GUATEMALAN GOVERNMENT, THROUGH THE MEDIUM OF
DIPLOMATS AND MILITARY OFFICERS, TO BACK PONCIANO'S CANDIDACY.
2. ON 22 NOVEMBER SANDOVAL PLANS TO GO FROM EL SALVADOR TO
MANAGUA, NICARAGUA, TO MEET PRIVATELY WITH BOBERTO ALEJOS ARZU,
QUATEMALAN EXILE RESIDENT IN MIAMI. THIS MEETING BETWEEN SANDOVAL
AND ALEJOS WAS AURANGED ON 18. NOVEMBER BY ALEJOS THROUGH THE FORMER
NICARAGUAN CONSUL IN MIAMI BY TELEPHONE TO SANDOVAL IN GUATEMALA CITY.
ALEJOS TOLD SANDOVAL THAT GENERAL SONOZA IJAD ASKED HIM TO COOPERATE
POLITICALLY AND FINANCIALLY WITH THE MUN DIRECTLY THIQUOH SANDOVAL.
IN MANAGUA ON 22 NOVEMBER SANDOVAL WILL REACH AN AGREEMENT WITH ALEJOS
IN FAVOR OF PONCIANO'S CANDIDACY.

CONSUL IN MIAMI, WIO IS INVOLVED IN A PLOT OT OVERVIEW WITH GEVERNMENT
VAD

TO AYASTASIO SONOZA. IN so DOING WILL TURN OVER FAIRLY SIZEABLE AMOUNT
OF AMMO CONSISTING 30 AND 50 CALIBER BULLETS, GRANADES AND SOUE MORTAR
SHEELS, ALSO FIVE CARBINES. BELIEVES TURNING OVER AMMO NECESSARY SINCE
CANNOT USE HIMSELF AND MOSTLY UNGUARDED CASES COULD KASILY CONSTITUTE
HAZARD TO LOCAL NATIVES NEAR BASES.

MEMORANDUM FOR THE RECORD
SUBJECT: AMBIDDY/1 Report on Nicaragua, and on General
Anastacio SOMOZA, and on Costa Rica
1. A/1 visited Washington and saw me on 14 and 15
October 1965. He visited Gen. SOMOZA at Johns Hopkins
Hospital is Baltimore the night of 15 October and called
me later to report on his meeting. The following items
were derived from his reports to me on these occasions:
a. Gen. SOMOZA has been in the hospital since
late September for a general physical check-up but
specifically for a special diet and treatane. The
question was that the report was not a single head no
musual problems, shows no evidence of neurosis or

and aggressive mental attitude. SOMOZA intends to

question was that they had by a lot of Indians also
mounted on horses and waving machetes in the air,
the other shows "Tachito" directing the National
Guard in Civic Action work building roads and
bridgesend helping them to get out of the
concerned. The third that Jack Vaughan opposes h' 4
election. When he gets out of the hospital
(estimated about 25 October), SOMOZA plans to run
a party at the Nic Embassy in Washington to which
Vaughan will have to come, and to confront him on
this point. SOMOZA is not worried about being
elected, with or without U.S. support. He says he
will not have to steal or buy the election either.

He has always been a friend of the U.S. and tried
to work with them, and will be very happy if they
will simply relax and try to live with him for a
few years. They may find out it will not be so
difficult as they seem to expect. On the other hand,
if the U.S. cuts his off, there are other countries
eager to fill the gap.
b. On the latter point (made about mid-
September 1965). A/1 followed up by clicitina: from

SCHICAGO.
6. Gen. SONOZA told A/1 that, when he met
